       <ul class="sub-menu menu-odd menu-depth-1">

        <h1 class="entry-title">
         Most Beautiful Places In The World
        </h1>
        <span class="author vcard hidden">
         <span class="fn">
          Dan
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="updated hidden">
         2010-10-11
        </span>
        <div class="vw-post-meta-wrapper vw-post-meta-large">
         <div class="vw-post-meta">
          <span class="vw-date-box vw-header-font ">
           <span class="vw-date-box-date">
            11
           </span>
           <span class="vw-date-box-month">
            <span>
             Oct
            </span>
            <span>
             2010
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <a class="vw-author-avatar" href="http://daddu.net/author/dan/" title="View all posts by Dan">
          </a>
          <a class="author-name author vw-header-font" href="http://daddu.net/author/dan/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Dan">
           Dan
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="vw-post-meta-icons">
          <a class="vw-post-meta-icon vw-post-comment-count" href="#comment">
           <i class="vw-icon icon-iconic-comment-alt2">
           </i>
           <span class="vw-header-font">
            588
           </span>
          </a>
          <a class="vw-post-meta-icon vw-post-likes-count " data-post-id="2857" href="#" id="vw-post-likes-id-2857" title="I like this">
           <i class="vw-icon icon-iconic-heart-empty">
           </i>
           <span class="vw-post-likes-number vw-header-font">
            1
           </span>
          </a>
          <a class="vw-post-share-count vw-post-meta-icon" href="#vw-post-shares-dialog">
           <i class="vw-icon icon-iconic-share">
           </i>
           <span class="vw-header-font vw-post-share-number">
            3
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="vw-featured-image">
         <a class="" href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/10/Swat12.jpg" rel="bookmark" title="Most Beautiful Places In The World">
          <img alt="Swat" class="attachment-vw_two_third_thumbnail_no_crop wp-post-image" height="400" itemprop="image" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/10/Swat12.jpg" width="600"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="pstads clearfix" style="margin-bottom:15px;">
         <script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js">
         </script>
         <!-- DadduResponsive -->
         <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-7563135538633152" data-ad-format="auto" data-ad-slot="6252216312" style="display:block">

          (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
         </script>

        <div class="vw-post-content clearfix">
         <h1>
          Edinburgh, Scotland
         </h1>
         <p>
          One of the most visited parts of the entire United Kingdom, Edinburgh is the capital city of Scotland and its beauty revolves largely around its interesting and intriguing history.
         </p>
         <p>
          Edinburgh Castle, for example, is a fortress built on the top of the Castle Rock volcano and can be dated back to the 11th century, whilst there is no doubting that the poems of famed poet Robert Burns were heavily influenced by the masses of scenery the city offers.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Edinburgh-Castle.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3113" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Edinburgh-Castle.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Edinburgh-Downtown.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3114" height="512" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Edinburgh-Downtown.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Edinburgh-Skyline.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3305" height="401" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Edinburgh-Skyline.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Burma, Asia
         </h1>
         <p>
          From 1044 onwards, the Barma started moving to the area from Tibet and once established, became prosperous due to trading to and from the area. It is during this time when the buildings were created that make Burma a place of beauty.
         </p>
         <p>
          To display the propserity of the area, a substanital amount of beautiful pagodas were built, many of which are still standing today and can be seen from miles away, scattered over the landscape.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Burma-Pagodas-Several.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3115" height="593" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Burma-Pagodas-Several.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Burma-Golden-Rock-Pagoda.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3116" height="513" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Burma-Golden-Rock-Pagoda.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Burma-Shwedagon-Pagoda.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3306" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Burma-Shwedagon-Pagoda.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Abu Simbel Temples, Egypt
         </h1>
         <p>
          There are several beautiful points of interest in Egypt and although the Abu Simbel Temples may not be as well known as the Great Pyramids of Giza or the Sphinx, they definitely rank highly in terms of sheer beauty.
         </p>
         <p>
          Originally carved into mountains in the 13th century BC, the two temples feature some staggering feats of construction, including four individual statues of Ramessess II, the Pharoah who the temples were created as a monument for, which each stand approximately 65 foot tall.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Abu-Simbel-Temples-Entrance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3117" height="545" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Abu-Simbel-Temples-Entrance.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Abu-Simbel-Temples-Statue.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3118" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Abu-Simbel-Temples-Statue.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Abu-Simbel-Temples-Small.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3307" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Abu-Simbel-Temples-Small.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Salar de Uyuni, Bolivia
         </h1>
         <p>
          Regarded as the worlds largest salt flat, the fact Salar de Uyuni is seen as being beautiful is because of both its unusual landscape and the amount of uncommon animals that inhabit the area.
         </p>
         <p>
          For instance, if you were to dig down into the surface of Salar de Uyuni, after the unusual salt-earth you would be greeted with a flowing river of brine. In addition, head to the area at the right time of year and you should expect to see culpeos, Bolivian vizcachas and the rare James flamingos.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Salar-de-Uyuni-Salt.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3119" height="435" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Salar-de-Uyuni-Salt.jpg" width="600"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Salar-de-Uyuni-Cacti.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3121" height="480" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Salar-de-Uyuni-Cacti.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Salar-de-Uyuni-Clear.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3123" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Salar-de-Uyuni-Clear.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Angkor, Cambodia
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          When Angkor was at its most populous in the thirteenth century, experts believe that it wasnt much smaller than the whole of Los Angeles. In 1431, however, almost all of the population left the city due to an invasion from the Ayutthaya kingdom.
         </p>
         <p>
          Today, it stands as a city of architectural, cultural and religious importance, shown by it being a UNESCO World Heritage site.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angkor-Buddhist-Monks.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3124" height="403" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angkor-Buddhist-Monks.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angkor-Bayonne.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3125" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angkor-Bayonne.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angkor-Wat-Statue.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3308" height="604" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angkor-Wat-Statue.jpg" width="453"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Las Vegas, Nevada, USA
         </h1>
         <p>
          There arent many better views of modern America than standing at the top of a hotel at either end of the famed Las Vegas strip and looking along it at night. The lights are glowing and brightening up the sky and the buzz once you actually enter the Strip is nothing short of electric.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Las-Vegas-Sunrise.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3126" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Las-Vegas-Sunrise.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Las-Vegas-Dusk.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3127" height="438" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Las-Vegas-Dusk.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Las-Vegas-Fremont-Street.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3309" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Las-Vegas-Fremont-Street.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Crazy Horse Memorial, South Dakota, USA
         </h1>
         <p>
          The largest monument in the world at the moment is the Spring Temple Buddha in China, which is 420 feet tall. However, once the Crazy Horse Memorial is completed, it will dwarf this by 140 feet.
         </p>
         <p>
          Started in 1948, the original sculptor Korczak Ziolkowski passed away in 1982, but his family remain heavily involved in the completion of the monument. With no specific end date planned, it is beautiful already, with simply Crazy Horses head protruding out of the Black Hills.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Crazy-Horse-Memorial-With-Model.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3128" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Crazy-Horse-Memorial-With-Model.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Crazy-Horse-Memorial-Head.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3129" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Crazy-Horse-Memorial-Head.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Crazy-Horse-Memorial-Distance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3130" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Crazy-Horse-Memorial-Distance.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Alexandria, Egypt
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Once home to one of the Seven Wonders of The World  the Lighthouse of Alexandria  as well as the largest ancient library in the world, the city today has a vast array of different archaeological sites that can be admired, such as Pompeys Pillar.
         </p>
         <p>
          In addition to the archaeological aspects, Alexandria boasts a plentiful amount of buildings, including the beautiful Al-Mursi Abul-Abbas mosque and the Bibliotehca Alexandria and various stunning monuments, such as Alexander the Great on Bucephalus.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alexandria-Pompeys-Pillar.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3310" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alexandria-Pompeys-Pillar.jpg" width="682"/>

         </p>

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Uxmal, Mexico
         </h1>
         <p>
          Like Machu Picchu in Peru, Uxmal is a site of pre-Colombian city ruins, but of the Maya civilization, rather than Inca, similar to Chichen Itza.
         </p>
         <p>
          Of the many astounding ruins that are available, the most beautiful is widely seen to be the Pyramid of the Magician, a pyramidial building that is 115 feet tall and unlike other similar Maya buildings, has rounded sides and is unusually steep.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Uxmal-Yucatan.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3132" height="518" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Uxmal-Yucatan.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Uxmal-Palacio-del-Gobernador.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3312" height="517" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Uxmal-Palacio-del-Gobernador.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Hawaii, USA
         </h1>
         <p>
          Although there are officially 137 islands in Hawaii, the largest 8 are the most populous, as well as arguably being the most stunning.
         </p>
         <p>
          Its difficult to choose one part of Hawaii to deem as the most beautiful, as the high peaks, clear waters and lush greenery, when combined with the hospitality of the locals, makes the entire area uniquely glorious.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hawaii-Annini-Beach-Sunrise.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3133" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hawaii-Annini-Beach-Sunrise.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hawaii-Hanakapiai-Beach.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3313" height="477" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hawaii-Hanakapiai-Beach.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Galapagos Islands, Ecuador
         </h1>
         <p>
          Located in the Pacific Ocean off the west coast of Ecuador are the Galapagos Islands, famed for being inhabited by many beautiful animals, as well as the sheer beauty of the islands themselves.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Galapagos Iguanas, for example, are possibly the areas most popular inhabitants, whilst the Blue-footed Booby is humorously pretty and both of them can be seen easily on many of the different islands.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Galapagos-Islands-Small.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3135" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Galapagos-Islands-Small.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Galapagos-Islands-Ocean.jpg">

          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          Plitvice Lakes, Croatia
         </h1>
         <p>
          The Plitvice Lakes are situated in Like, a mountainous area of Croatia and can be divided up into 16 individual lakes, all of which flow into the Korana River.
         </p>
         <p>
          Croatia may have some fantastic cities like Dubrovnik, but arguably the best view in the whole country is watching the water pour over the side of the mountain and down the face of the many travertines and caves of the Plitvice Lakes.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Plitvice-Lakes-Waterfalls.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3136" height="518" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Plitvice-Lakes-Waterfalls.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Plitvice-Lakes-Bridge.jpg">

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Aeolian Islands, Italy
         </h1>
         <p>
          Dating back thousands of years, the Aeolian Islands are a collection of small islands that are one of Italys most notable areas of natural beauty.
         </p>
         <p>
          What attracts 200,000 people each summer to the Aeolian Islands is more than just the fact they are beautiful, but that they hold a very admirable rustic charm, taking anyone who visits back to a way of life that is centuries old.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Aeolian-Islands-Ocean.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3316" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Aeolian-Islands-Ocean.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Aeolian-Islands-Lipari.jpg">

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Alhambra, Spain
         </h1>
         <p>
          Designed and constructed in the 14th century to be the home of one of Spains Muslim Kings, it was used more as a residence for Charles V, a Holy Roman Emperor in the 16th century.
         </p>
         <p>
          Uninhabited for several hundred years, it was rediscovered throghout the 1800s and further to restorations, is now one of the most beautiful buildsing in Spain, featuring some particularly intricate internal art work.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alhambra-Mountains.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3139" height="406" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alhambra-Mountains.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alhambra-Distance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3321" height="540" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alhambra-Distance.jpg" width="720"/>
          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Alhambra-Moors-Tears.jpg">

          </a>
         </h1>
         <h1>
          White Cliffs of Dover, England
         </h1>
         <p>
          The White Clifs of Dover are famed for being just that  beautifully white cliffs on the coast of Dover, easily viewable from the opposite French coast.
         </p>
         <p>
          However, the cliffs are also packed with interesting history, as inside them there are dozens of tunnels, initially created in the Middle Ages. Used largely throughout the Napoleonic Wars, they were also used in the Second World War, with Winston Churchill having a residence within the cliffs.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/White-Cliffs-of-Dover-Ocean.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3140" height="496" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/White-Cliffs-of-Dover-Ocean.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/White-Cliffs-of-Dover-Side1.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3142" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/White-Cliffs-of-Dover-Side1.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>

          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Nile River, Ethiopia / Sudan / Egypt / Uganda / Democratic Republic of Congo
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          If you were only able to visit one river in your life, whilst there are some beautiful stretches of water earth, many would find it difficult to not choose the Nile.
         </p>
         <p>
          Stretching for 6,650 kilometres, the Nile runs through five countries and four cities and what you would see were you to travel along its entire length makes the Nile a worthy inclusion in any list of the most beautiful places in the world.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Nile-Sunset1.jpg">

         <h1>
          <strong>
           Angel Falls, Venezuela
          </strong>
         </h1>
         <p>
          There have been several waterfalls included in this list, all of which are breathtaking. Angel Falls, whilst not being the most popular, is considered to be one of the most beautiful.
         </p>
         <p>
          The worlds highest waterfall at 3,212 feet tall, the water that comes over the top of the mountain falls for 2,647 feet before plunging into the Kerep River below.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angel-Falls-Distance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3148" height="480" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angel-Falls-Distance.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angel-Falls-Close.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3149" height="1024" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angel-Falls-Close.jpg" width="681"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Angel-Falls-Misty.jpg">

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Mont Saint-Michel, France
         </h1>
         <p>
          What was once a small tidal island off the coast of northern France began its transformation in the 6th century, acting as a stronghold for the Romano-British.
         </p>
         <p>
          It wasnt until the 8th century when the first religious building was constructed on the site and from that point forward it continued to grow in both stature and importance.
         </p>
         <p>
          Whats interesting about Mont Saint-Michel is that after the monastery supported William of Normandy claim the English throne in 1047, they were given a small island just off the Cornish coast. Building a replica island, St Michaels Mount in Penzance is one of the areas most stunning attractions in Cornwall.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Mont-St-Michel-Houses.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3326" height="800" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Mont-St-Michel-Houses.jpg" width="533"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Mont-St-Michel-Road.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3327" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Mont-St-Michel-Road.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Mont-St-Michel-Distance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3328" height="512" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Mont-St-Michel-Distance.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Olympia, Greece
         </h1>
         <p>
          Home to the very first Olympic games, which historians believe could have taken place earlier than 776 BC, Olympia was made a redundant area after 394 AD, when Theodosius I permanently suspended the games.
         </p>
         <p>
          Visiting the site today, many people simply stand and attempt to take in what the atmosphere must have been like over 2,000 years ago. With various remains to see, including the Philippeion, the stadium and the exedra, the area in which the judges were seated, the whole area is awe-inspiring.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Olympia-Philippeion.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3329" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Olympia-Philippeion.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Olympia-Leonidaion-Columns.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3330" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Olympia-Leonidaion-Columns.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Olympia-Ruins.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3331" height="403" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Olympia-Ruins.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          New England, USA
         </h1>
         <p>
          Covering the entire north east region of the United States of America, it is generally accepted that the states encompassed within the New England umbrella phrase are Maine, New Hampshire, Vermont, Massachusetts, Rhode Island and Connecticut.
         </p>
         <p>
          Beautiful the year round, it is in September and October when the area is at its best, with the orange and red colours of the trees seeming to be like nothing seen elsewhere on earth.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/New-England-Trees.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3341" height="479" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/New-England-Trees.jpg" width="717"/>

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Stonehenge, England
         </h1>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          For centuries there has been much debate as to when Stonehenge dates back to and what its actual use was.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          With experts believing Stonehenge dates back to the Neolithic period and with theories varying considerably, there isnt much doubt that Stonehenge is anything but a beautiful eye-opener to historic construction.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Stonehenge-Entirety.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3332" height="536" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Stonehenge-Entirety.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Stonehenge-Heelstone.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3333" height="1024" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Stonehenge-Heelstone.jpg" width="683"/>

          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Stonehenge-Sun.jpg">

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Big Ben and the Houses of Parliament, London
         </h1>
         <p>
          Whilst London itself has already been mentioned in this list, most would agree that Big Ben and The Houses of Parliament deserve their own place, purely for their iconic British status.
         </p>
         <p>
          Situated on the bank of the River Thames, the Houses of Parliament is where the House of Commons and House of Lords meets, whilst Big Ben, now into its 151st year of operation, is the worlds third highest freestanding clock tower at 315.9 feet tall.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Big-Ben-and-Houses-of-Parliament-River-Thames.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3367" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Big-Ben-and-Houses-of-Parliament-River-Thames.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Big-Ben-and-Houses-of-Parliament-Night.jpg">

          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Serengeti, Africa
         </h1>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          Spanning an area of over 30,000 square kilometres, the Serengeti is the home of the most expansive overland migration on earth.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          With hundreds of individual animal species crossing the Serengeti every year, the migration of the wildebeests, zebras and buffalos is one of the most wonderful sights of nature in the world.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Serengeti-Wildebeest-and-Zebra-Migration.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3335" height="512" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Serengeti-Wildebeest-and-Zebra-Migration.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Serengeti-Zebra-Migration.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3336" height="477" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Serengeti-Zebra-Migration.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Serengeti-Sunset.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3337" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Serengeti-Sunset.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Antarctica
         </h1>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          Covered almost entirely by ice, the average thickness of which is approximately 1.6 kilometres thick, Antarctica is the fifth largest continent in the world.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          Considering the area is as cold as it is, its surprising to hear that there are dozens of animals that call Antarctica home  and up 5,000 people, albeit on a temporary basis.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Antarctica-Iceberg.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3338" height="569" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Antarctica-Iceberg.jpg" width="720"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Antarctica-Cliffs.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3339" height="473" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Antarctica-Cliffs.jpg" width="720"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Antarctica-Peninsula.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3340" height="432" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Antarctica-Peninsula.jpg" width="650"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Altiplano, South America
         </h1>
         <p>
          Originally an area of land covered entirely by Lake Ballivan, it has drained over time and is now an area of outstanding natural beauty.
         </p>
         <p>
          Encompassing areas such as Salar de Uyuni, Altiplano is simply a stunning part of the globe.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Altiplano-Mountain-and-Water.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3345" height="489" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Altiplano-Mountain-and-Water.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Altiplano-Orange-Colours.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3346" height="486" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Altiplano-Orange-Colours.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Altiplano-Greenery.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3347" height="494" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Altiplano-Greenery.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Hagia Sophia, Istanbul, Turkey
         </h1>
         <p>
          Originally built as a cathedral for over 10 centuries until 1453, when it was a most for just under 500 years, Hagia Sophia is now a famous museum in Istanbul, Turkeys biggest city.
         </p>
         <p>
          A stunning piece of architectural beauty, Hagia Sophia is beautiful on the outside and even more breathtaking when you walk through the entrance.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hagia-Sophia-Towers-and-Dome.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3348" height="451" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hagia-Sophia-Towers-and-Dome.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hagia-Sophia-Internal.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3349" height="922" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hagia-Sophia-Internal.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hagia-Sophia-Night.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3350" height="479" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hagia-Sophia-Night.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Carlsbad Caverns, New Mexico
         </h1>
         <p>
          Encompassed within the Carlsbad Caverns National Park in the Guadalupe Mountains, the caverns are located deep within the mountains and ground, with the most popular cavern being 750 feet below ground level.
         </p>
         <p>
          Consisting of different rooms, such as the Balloon Ballroom, The Hall of the Giants and the Kings Palace, each and every cavern in the Carlsbad Caverns is truly wonderful.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Carlsbad-Caverns-Hall-of-Giants.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3351" height="475" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Carlsbad-Caverns-Hall-of-Giants.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          <strong>
           <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Carlsbad-Caverns-Lower-Cave.jpg">
            <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3352" height="475" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Carlsbad-Caverns-Lower-Cave.jpg" width="717"/>
           </a>
          </strong>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Potala Palace, Tibet
         </h1>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          Now transformed into one of Chinas most popular museums, Potala Palace was once the permanent residence of the Dalai Lama, up until 1959 when the then Dalai Lama travelled to India further to a potentially devstating uprising.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: left;">
          A particularly impenetrable building, Potala Palace has copper-poured foundations, walls that are in excess of 16 feet thick and has thirteen stories containing over 200,000 statues in 1,000 rooms.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Potala-Palace-Distance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3354" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Potala-Palace-Distance.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Potala-Palace-Morning.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3355" height="518" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Potala-Palace-Morning.jpg" width="691"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Potala-Palace-Stairs.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3356" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Potala-Palace-Stairs.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Hassan II Mosque, Casablanca, Morocco
         </h1>
         <p>
          The largest mosque in the whole of Morocco, the Hassan II Mosque was designed by Michael Pinseau and further to its completion in 1993, can house 105,000 people at once, with 25,000 able to be in the actual central mosque area itself.
         </p>
         <p>
          Having the tallest minaret on earth just under 690 feet tall, the mosque required a combination of 12,500 builders and artists 3 years to construct.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hassan-II-Mosque-Tower.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3357" height="538" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hassan-II-Mosque-Tower.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hassan-II-Mosque-Fountain-and-Wall.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3358" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hassan-II-Mosque-Fountain-and-Wall.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hassan-II-Mosque-Internal.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3359" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Hassan-II-Mosque-Internal.jpg" width="717"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <h1>
          Sagrada Familia, Barcelona, Spain
         </h1>
         <div>
          Officially known as the Temple Expiatori de le Sagrada Familia (which when translated into English means Expiatory Church of the Holy Family), building work started in 1882 and although it isnt expected to be finished until 2026, a small section of the building is supposed to be opened to the public in September 2010.
         </div>
         <div>
          A completely privately funded Roman Catholic church, the Sagrada Familia has long been one of Barcelonas most popular tourist attractions since Antoni Gaudi started designing and constructing the building almost 130 years ago.
         </div>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Sagrada-Familia-Nativity-Facade.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3360" height="478" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Sagrada-Familia-Nativity-Facade.jpg" width="720"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Sagrada-Familia-Distance.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3361" height="477" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Sagrada-Familia-Distance.jpg" width="720"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Sagrada-Familia-Towers.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-3362" height="900" src="http://daddu.net/wp-content/uploads/2010/05/Sagrada-Familia-Towers.jpg" width="629"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>

         <!-- #comment-## -->
         <li class="comment even thread-even depth-1" id="li-comment-21430">
          <div class="comment-body clearfix" id="comment-21430">
           <div class="comment-text">
            <div class="author">
             <div class="author-name vw-header-font">
              Malcolm Hutton
             </div>
             <div class="date">
              December 23, 2011 at 3:17 pm							 
              <a aria-label="Reply to Malcolm Hutton" class="comment-reply-link" href="/most-beautiful-places-in-the-world/3/?replytocom=21430#respond" onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-21430", "21430", "respond", "2857" )'>
               Reply
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text">
             <p>
              The title should perhaps be the Most Breathtaking Places.    They are not all accessible for most of us.
             </p>
             <p>
              I didnt spot Cairns, yet this has to be Paradise on Earth.    The surroundings are both beautiful and some have that breathtaking quality.      Where else is there a railway station like Kuranda which is full of tropical growth?    Then Mosman Gorge has a mind relaxing tranquility in the rainforest with a river plunging over boulders, and Baron Gorge is into the breathtaking category.   The Strangler Fig Trees take on wonderful shapes, one like a Cathedral.     Next there is Cascade Falls with more peace for the mind, and then the stunning coastal road winding around the cliff edges from Cairns to Port Douglas overlooking a clear crystal Sea behind the Reef which is so transparent one can see the sandy floor.   The Reef itself is a maze of colour and home to the most beautifully coloured fish.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>

             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text">
             <p>
              Awesome pictures., but you should really check your facts before you post them.  Washington D.C. is just that.District of Columbia (which you spelled wrong, and yes it matters), not Washington D.C., Colombia, U.S.A.  Also, Mt. Everest is NOT the largest above-water mountain on Earth; Denali (Mt. McKinley) is.  Mt. Everest is approximatley only 17,000 feet tall from its base on the Tibetan Plateau, which is already at about 12,000 feet.  Denali is over 18,000 feet tall from its base, and also much larger by sheer mass.  So your wording should have said the tallest or highest mountain in the world.  And technically, the island of Hawaii is the largest mountain.  Very cool pictures, though.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>

              This is an outstanding collection of pictures and facts. I was quite disappointed to find that Canada had not made it on your list. Canada has some of the most beautiful places on the planet. There are places like Lake Jasper, Banff, Lake Louise, the Hopewell Rocks, the Confederation Bridge, and so much more. Every province and territory here in Canada has so much beautiful sights. I personally have seen breathtaking scenery such as a sunrise in the northern part of Ontario where is untouched land and lakes.
             </p>

         <li class="pingback odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1" id="li-comment-50720">
          <div class="comment-body clearfix" id="comment-50720">
           <div class="comment-text">
            <div class="author">
             <div class="author-name vw-header-font">
              <a class="url" href="http://amazingplacestoseebeforeyoudie.com/?p=71" rel="external nofollow">
               Amazing Places to See Before You Die | Iguazu Falls, Brazil-Argentina Border
              </a>
             </div>
             <div class="date">
              September 15, 2012 at 2:27 pm							 
              <a aria-label="Reply to Amazing Places to See Before You Die | Iguazu Falls, Brazil-Argentina Border" class="comment-reply-link" href="/most-beautiful-places-in-the-world/3/?replytocom=50720#respond" onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-50720", "50720", "respond", "2857" )'>
               Reply
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text">
             <p>
              [] There are many different large and popular waterfalls all around the world, but none offer as spectacular views as Iguazu Falls does.Sat on the border between Brazil and Argentina, it is possible to get safely into Iguazu Falls that you can benefit from over 250 degrees worth of waterfalls surrounding you. It may not be as big as some of the other waterfalls around the world, but Iguazu Falls is by far one of the most stunning.source:
              <a href="http://daddu.net/most-beautiful-places-in-the-world/" rel="nofollow">
               http://daddu.net/most-beautiful-places-in-the-world/
              </a>
              []
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>

         <li class="pingback odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1" id="li-comment-50852">
          <div class="comment-body clearfix" id="comment-50852">
           <div class="comment-text">
            <div class="author">
             <div class="author-name vw-header-font">
              <a class="url" href="http://www.gofinland.org/finnish-likes-and-dislikes/" rel="external nofollow">
               Finnish Likes and Dislikes | Go Finland
              </a>
             </div>
             <div class="date">
              January 9, 2013 at 9:33 am							 
              <a aria-label="Reply to Finnish Likes and Dislikes | Go Finland" class="comment-reply-link" href="/most-beautiful-places-in-the-world/3/?replytocom=50852#respond" onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-50852", "50852", "respond", "2857" )'>
               Reply
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text">
             <p>
              [] Finns like to spend their vacation in a small cottage at a lake. Considering the huge number of lakes in Finland, its no surprise that almost every Finn has a cottage at a lake. All cottages have saunas (naturally!). You might want to adopt this habit for your vacation as well. If youre not traveling in winter, Finnish countryside is one of the most beautiful scenes in the world. []
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>

             <p>
              beautiful collection ,scenes,awesomes its my desire that i see these pray me nd guide me if possible
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </li>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   (function() {
				function addSubmittedClassToFormContainer(e) {
					var form = e.target.form.parentNode;
					var className = 'mc4wp-form-submitted';
					(form.classList) ? form.classList.add(className) : form.className += ' ' + className;
				}

				function hideHoneypot(h) {
					var n = document.createElement('input');
					n.type = 'hidden';
					n.name = h.name;
					n.style.display = 'none';
					n.value = h.value;
					h.parentNode.replaceChild(n,h);
				}

				var forms = document.querySelectorAll('.mc4wp-form');
				for (var i = 0; i &lt; forms.length; i++) {
					(function(f) {

						// make sure honeypot is hidden
						var h = f.querySelector('input[name="_mc4wp_required_but_not_really"]');
						if(h) {
							hideHoneypot(h);
						}

						// add class on submit
						var b = f.querySelector('[type="submit"]');
						if(b.addEventListener) {
							b.addEventListener('click', addSubmittedClassToFormContainer);
						} else {
							b.attachEvent('click', addSubmittedClassToFormContainer);
						}

					})(forms[i]);
				}
			})();
  </script>
